<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、損減事2　宇一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科損減事，說明引生見煩惱的損減事，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出四種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">損減事亦有四種。一、謗因，二、謗果，三、謗作用，四、謗善事。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　引生見煩惱的損減事也有如上所說謗因、謗果、謗作用、謗善事四種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇二、隨釋4　宙一、謗因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接下來各別解釋什麼稱為謗因、謗果、謗作用、謗善事，分四科；第一科謗因，說明謗因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此中，謂無施與乃至無妙行、惡行，是名謗因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知，認為布施沒有功德，愛養祠祀也沒有功德，不用去祭祀祖先等，乃至妙好的善行不能得樂果，下劣的惡行不能得苦果，善惡不分，這類損減事實真相，於因的錯誤知見，名謗因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宙二、謗果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科謗果，說明何謂謗果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂無妙行、惡行業果異熟，是名謗果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　認為善行不能得可愛的異熟果，惡行不能得不可愛的苦果，這類於果的錯誤的知見，名謗果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宙三、謗作用4　洪一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科謗作用，說明謗作用的內涵，分四科；第一科標，標示出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4426"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂無此世間乃至無化生有情，名謗作用。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是外道對禪定所現的境界無知錯解，或依尋伺思惟，認為沒有此世間、彼世間、無父無母、乃至無化生有情（中有）、這一類對諸法各有作用撥無的損減執，名為謗作用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">洪二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為何如此說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">洪三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸士夫用是此中作用義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　士夫用，士夫就是人，人的作用就是這裡的作用義。外道認為，人沒有從此世間投生到另一個世間的作用，也沒有中陰身等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">洪四、廣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科廣，詳細說明士夫用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此士夫用復有四種。一、往來用，二、持胎藏用，三、置種子用，四、後有業用。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這士夫用又有四種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、往來用：未斷煩惱的凡夫，在三界來來往往，從此世間往彼世間受生，不斷輪迴；外道則認為沒有往來，沒有此世間、沒有彼世間。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、持胎藏用：有情投胎時，母親有任持胎藏的作用，外道撥無此事，認為無母。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、置種子用：有情投胎時，父親有置種子的作用，外道撥無此事，認為無父。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、後有業用：欲色二界有情於死後有中陰身傳持隨業識投生後有，外道認為沒有中有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道撥無這四種人的作用，名謗作用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宙四、謗善事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科謗善事，說明謗善事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若謂世間無阿羅漢等，名謗善事。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若執著世間沒有真阿羅漢，沒有修行證果，沒有三寶四諦，沒有這些善法的事，名謗善事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂無施與等者：此中諸義，如有尋有伺地廣說應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/08.htm#43354:6017">陵本八卷十四頁612</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處所說無施與等的義理，在〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8，252頁有詳細說明應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4427"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、能依見2　黃一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科能依見，說明能依的見煩惱，分二科；第一科標，標出由所依事生五見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依此廣略八事、二事，生於五見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止廣的八事，或者是略的二種事，能引生五種見煩惱。廣是指四種增益事及四種損減事，合起來有八事；略是指增益事及損減事二種，合說廣略八事、二事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出五種見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂薩迦耶見、邊執見、見取、戒禁取、邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依此廣略八事、二事能引生薩迦耶見的我見、身見；斷常二見的邊執見；於生天方便增益，執非方便為方便的戒禁取見；執著於身見、邊見、邪見、以劣為勝等非理之見的見取見；及於解脫方便增益，執非方便為方便、方便為非方便的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依此廣略八事二事者：前說八事，謂增益事有四種，損減事亦有四種，是名為廣。又說二事，一、增益事，二、損減事，是名為略。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說八事，指增益事有四種，損減事也有四種，說名為廣。又說二事，一、增益事，二、損減事，說名為略。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、依六十二事生2　地一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依六十二事生，說明依六十二事生邊執見及邪見，分二科；第一科標，標示出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又依六十二事，生邊執見及邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止六十二種事，能引種種的邊執見：斷見、常見等，以及邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂計前際事、計後際事，如經廣說。依此事差別，有六十二見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　指依前生、來生的依正二報等事，產生種種見執，如經上廣說。依前後生有情事及器世間事生出種種虛妄分別與執著，而有六十二見。如《梵網六十二見經》、《大智度論》、《大毘婆沙論》、及〈攝事分〉卷87等有詳細說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂計前際事等者：攝事分說：又諸外道，薩迦耶見以為根本，有六十二諸惡見趣。謂四常見論、四一分常見論、二無因論、四有邊無邊想論、四不死矯亂論，如是十八諸惡見趣，是計前際說我論者。又有十六有想見論、八無想論、八非有想非無想論、七斷見論、五現法涅槃論，此四十四諸惡見趣，是計後際說我論者。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/87.htm#43366:66235">陵本八十七卷二頁6558</a>）此應準知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈攝事分〉卷87說，又諸外道以薩迦耶見（我見）為根本，展轉引生六十二見；其中四常見論、四一分常見論、二無因論、四有邊無邊想論、四不死矯亂論，如是十八種諸惡見趣，是執著前生之我見而引生的邪見；又有十六有想見論、八無想論、八非有想非無想論、七斷見論、五現法涅槃論，這四十四種諸惡見趣，是執著來生之我見而引生的邪見，如是執著前生我見而引生的十八種諸惡見與執著來生之我見而引生的四十四種諸惡見共六十二見。在本論卷87，2584頁有說到，此處應準照那裡的解釋即可了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥六、疑煩惱攝2　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科疑煩惱攝，說明疑煩惱之所依事等，分二科；第一科標，標出依六事生疑。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4428"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">疑依六事生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　疑依止六件事情而產生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出疑所依的六事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、聞不正法，二、見師邪行，三、見所信受意見差別，四、性自愚魯，五、甚深法性，六、廣大法教。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、聞不正法：聽聞不正法，心裡會生起懷疑。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、見師邪行：看到所學習的老師有錯誤的行為。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、見所信受意見差別：對所信受的法，有不同意見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、性自愚魯：自己本身的資質愚痴弩鈍，不明白所聽聞的法，所以生疑。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、甚深法性：對於因為自己沒有辦法證到的甚深法性，也會生疑。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、廣大法教：對於佛說的廣大法教，因為沒有辦法學習，也會生起疑惑。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》聞不正法等者：由聞不正法故，於法生疑；見師邪行故，於師生疑；見所信受意見差別故，於學生疑；性自愚魯故，於誨生疑；甚深法性故，於證生疑；廣大法教故，於教生疑。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為聽聞到不正法，對法產生懷疑；看到老師作錯誤事情，對老師生起懷疑；見老師教的道理，自己與老師的意見不一樣，對於所學的道理生起疑惑；自己比較愚笨不聰明，因為聽不懂，對於老師的教誨也會生起懷疑；對於甚深法性，因為沒有證到那個境界，也會於證生疑，會覺得有可能嗎？有可能作到這件事情嗎？對於廣大法教，因為沒有辦法學習，也會生起疑惑。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉七、差別2　戌一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科差別，根本煩惱的九相，第七相差別，說明不善法的差別相，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="47772:43374"></a>問：何等名為煩惱差別？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：煩惱的差別有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、答2　亥一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標，標出有十五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：一切差別，略有十五。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：煩惱的差別可以要略歸納成十五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出十五種煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4429"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、內門煩惱，二、外門煩惱，三、見斷煩惱，四、修斷煩惱，五、可愛趣纏所攝煩惱，六、非可愛趣纏所攝煩惱，七、隨眠所攝煩惱，八、軟品煩惱，九、中品煩惱，十、上品煩惱，十一、散亂位煩惱，十二、諫悔位煩惱，十三、羸劣位煩惱，十四、制伏位煩惱，十五、離繫位煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、內門煩惱：內六處眼耳鼻舌身意，是六個門，很多消息會從眼耳鼻舌身意進來，稱內六處為門。依六根取境，根境和合生識，由此引生虛妄分別之各種煩惱，名內門煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、外門煩惱：色聲香味觸法外六處，也是引起煩惱的六道門，因為色聲香味觸法引生的煩惱，名外門煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、見斷煩惱：初見聖道所要斷除的煩惱，於欲界、色界、無色界苦集滅道等引生的分別起的愛見煩惱，總共有一百一十二種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、修斷煩惱：修道位所斷除俱生起的煩惱，欲界有俱生起的薩迦耶見、邊執見、貪、恚、慢、無明六種；色無色界對治修中除了瞋，各有五種煩惱，三界合起來有十六種煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、可愛趣纏所攝煩惱：可愛趣指是人天的處所，屬於人天處的煩惱，名可愛趣纏所攝煩惱，通常以貪欲為主要煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、非可愛趣纏所攝煩惱：屬三惡道所攝的煩惱，名非可愛趣纏所攝煩惱，以瞋為主要煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、隨眠所攝煩惱：指煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、軟品煩惱：軟品是指最後斷、最微細難斷的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、中品煩惱：屬於中等強度的煩惱，次要斷的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、上品煩惱：是指最先斷、最粗顯的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十一、散亂位煩惱：還沒有發心出家受戒者之煩惱、或欲界的煩惱，欲界眾生都是散心的，沒有定，欲界的煩惱屬於散亂位煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二、諫悔位煩惱：指出家受戒後，所有犯戒為他人所諫舉，而生追悔的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十三、羸劣位煩惱：指修五停心觀；多貪眾生不淨觀，多瞋眾生慈悲觀，多癡眾生緣起觀，散亂眾生數息觀，多慢眾生界分別觀，所需調伏的上品煩惱。《瑜伽論記》卷15說：「至老病時所起煩惱，名羸劣位煩惱。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十四、制伏位煩惱：指得定調伏的煩惱，如初禪要制伏尋伺欲，二禪要制伏初禪的尋伺不寂靜；三禪要制伏二禪的喜；四禪要制伏三禪的樂，要制伏這些煩惱才能得定，這些煩惱名制伏位煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十五、離繫位煩惱：成就聖道遠離煩惱種子的繫縛名離繫位，離繫位所要斷除的煩惱，包括見所斷及修所斷的煩惱等二大類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉八、得失2　戌一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科得失，根本煩惱的九種相貌，第八相得失，說明煩惱的得失，分二科；第一科標，標出煩惱全無功德，唯有眾多過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="47338:43382"></a>復次，煩惱無有功德，有多過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，煩惱都沒有功德，只有很多過失。只要生起煩惱就有過失，談不上有什麼功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋煩惱無功有過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂於纏位汙心相續，廣說如有尋有伺地。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱數數現行名纏，未斷煩惱的凡夫，煩惱數數現行，使令染污心相續不斷，引生種種過患，詳細情形如〈有尋有伺地〉所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉九、能所治2　戌一、簡非能治2　亥一、標義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科能所治，根本煩惱的九種相貌，最後一相能所治，約能治與所治，說明煩惱唯是所治，分二科；第一科簡非能治，簡別煩惱本身不能對治煩惱，又分二科；第一科標義，標出煩惱不能對治煩惱的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，煩惱非能對治。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，不能用煩惱來對治煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、會違</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科會違（相違），說明善法與煩惱，性質不同才能互相對治。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">雖復經言：依愛斷愛、依慢斷慢。然非煩惱；但是善心加行希求高舉行相，與彼相似，假說愛、慢。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　雖然經上有時候說，依止著愛可以斷除愛，依止著慢可以斷除慢，可是能斷的愛與慢不是煩惱，只是發動善心時，希望能夠斷除愛與慢，這能斷的善心與所斷的愛與慢相似，就假說此能斷的善心為愛與慢。如《雜阿含經》卷21：佛說什麼稱作依愛斷愛呢？是指聖弟子聽聞某位尊者、某尊者弟子盡諸有漏，乃至自知不受後有。心想自己為何不盡諸有漏，乃至自知不受後有。這麼一想於盡諸有漏，乃至自知不受後有的功德生起強大的愛樂心，因此精進修行，而斷諸有漏，乃至自知不受後有，是名依愛斷愛。此愛彼愛相似但作用不同，假名為愛。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又說什麼稱作依慢斷慢？指聖弟子聽聞某位尊者、某尊者弟子盡諸有漏，無漏心解脫、慧解脫，現法自知作證：「我生已盡，梵行已立，所作已作，自知不受後有。」聽聞之後，作念：「彼聖弟子盡諸有漏，乃至自知不受後有。我現在為何不盡諸有漏，何故不自知不受後有。」內心生起彼既丈夫我亦爾的高舉心，依此而斷諸有漏，乃至自知不受後有，是名依慢斷慢。表面上看都是慢，但此慢乃趣向聖道之善法欲，由此而斷慢煩惱，假說以慢斷慢。又如依善法欲離欲稱為以欲斷欲，雖然都是欲，但善法欲屬善法所攝，所斷的欲屬不善法所攝，性質不同才有對治作用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4430"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、顯是所治</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯是所治，顯示煩惱是所對治的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，如前說十五種心對治差別，當知煩惱是彼所治，亦十五種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如前文所說有十五種心能對治煩惱的善法，應當了知煩惱是這些善法所對治的，也有十五種。厭患對治能對治內門煩惱；斷對治能對治外門煩惱；持對治能對治見斷煩惱；遠分對治能對治修斷煩惱；所欲趣纏對治能對治可愛趣纏所攝煩惱；非所欲趣纏對治能對治非可愛趣纏所攝煩惱故；隨眠對治能對治隨眠所攝煩惱；軟品煩惱對治能對治細微的軟品煩惱；中品煩惱對治能對治中品煩惱；上品煩惱對治能對治上品煩惱；散亂對治能對治散亂位煩惱，諫悔對治能對治諫悔位煩惱；羸劣對治能對治羸劣位煩惱，制伏對治能對治制伏位煩惱，離繫對治能對治離繫位煩惱。善惡性質不同，以善治惡，有所治的惡法就有能治的善法，能所相對，能所皆無實自性，然皆有如幻的作用，仔細思惟諸法的自相、共相，就能趣向第一義諦，不離假名而超越假名。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、隨煩惱2　酉一、顯差別4　戌一、依處2　亥一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨煩惱，再來說隨煩惱，隨著根本煩惱而現起的隨煩惱。隨煩惱有大隨、中隨、及小隨三類，定義不同，分二科；第一科顯差別，顯示隨煩惱的種種差別相，又分四科；第一科依處，說明隨煩惱的依止處，又分二科；第一科標，標出隨煩惱的依止處有九種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，隨煩惱依處，當知略有九種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，隨煩惱的依止處，要略而言有九種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出九種隨煩惱的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、展轉共住，二、展轉相舉，三、利養，四、邪命，五、不敬尊師，六、不忍，七、毀增上戒，八、毀增上心，九、毀增上慧。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、展轉共住：出家眾一起共住於身業、語業、意業、見解、戒律、及利養恭敬，不能和合時，容易引生忿、恨的煩惱，乃至產生粗暴的身語表業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、展轉相舉：出家眾共住，若有人犯戒生起覆藏的煩惱，不欲人知，此時若有人舉罪就可能惱羞成怒。因此在犯戒及彼此展轉舉罪時，容易引生覆、惱的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、利養：對於他人得到利養，心不能忍，以此引生嫉妒的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、邪命：用不正當的方法取得生活所需稱為邪命。比如《雜阿含經》卷18：尊者舍利弗說：「姊妹！諸所有沙門、婆羅門明於事者、明於橫法、邪命求食者、如是沙門、婆羅門下口食也。若諸沙門、婆羅門仰觀星曆，邪命求食者，如是沙門、婆羅門則為仰口食也。若諸沙門、婆羅門為他使命，邪命求食者，如是沙門、婆羅門則為方口食也。若有沙門、婆羅門為諸醫方種種治病，邪命求食者，如是沙門、婆羅門則為維口食也。姊妹！我不墮此四種邪命而求食也。然我，姊妹！但以法求食而自活也，是故我說不為四種食也。」對出家眾而言不應依下口食、仰口食、方口食、維口食等四種邪命而食，而應如法求食。而在家人也不應以誑、諂之心謀利而食。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、不敬尊師：若人貢高我慢不敬尊師，此時能生憍逸的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、不忍：於眾生心無悲愍，不能堪忍對方的身語二業，能引發傷害逼惱有情的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、毀增上戒：毀犯戒律時，有無慚及無愧的隨煩惱生起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、毀增上心，及九、毀增上慧：有十二種隨煩惱心所生起；包括惛沈、掉舉、不信、懈怠、放逸、忘念、散亂、不正知、惡作、睡眠、尋、伺，這些都是障礙定慧的心所。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、自性2　亥一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科自性，說明隨煩惱的自性，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="46825:43397"></a>復次，隨煩惱自性云何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，隨煩惱的體性是怎麼樣呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋2　天一、出種類3　地一、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科出種類，說明隨煩惱的種類，又分三科；第一科列，列出隨煩惱的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂忿、恨、覆、惱、嫉、慳、誑、諂、憍、害、無慚、無愧、惛沈、掉舉、不信、懈怠、放逸、忘念、散亂、不正知、惡作、睡眠、尋、伺。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨煩惱包括：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　小隨煩惱：忿、恨、覆、惱、嫉、慳、誑、諂、憍、害，</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　中隨煩惱：無慚、無愧，</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　大隨煩惱：惛沈、掉舉、不信、懈怠、放逸、忘念、散亂、不正知，</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不定心所：惡作、睡眠、尋、伺等心所法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4431"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、指</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科指，指出〈本地分‧意地〉已說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如本地分已廣宣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如〈本地分‧意地〉卷1中已經說過五十三個心所的名字。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等類，名隨煩惱自性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說，名隨煩惱自性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如本地分已廣宣說者：謂本地分意地助伴，已廣宣說差別名故。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/01.htm#43406:322">陵本一卷十頁40</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧意地〉的助伴心所，已詳細宣說隨煩惱的差別名。如卷1，18頁中所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、配依處2　地一、別配屬</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科配依處，將隨煩惱配屬九種依處說明，分二科；第一科別配屬，將隨煩惱各別配屬九種依處說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中初二，依初依處而生；第三、第四，依第二；第五、第六，依第三；第七、第八，依第四；第九，依第五；第十，依第六；十一、十二，依第七；所餘十二，依後二依處而生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於隨煩惱中最初二種忿及恨，依止初處的展轉共住而生；第三的覆與第四的惱，依止第二的展轉相舉而生；第五的嫉及第六的慳，依止第三的利養而生；第七的誑與第八的諂，依第四邪命而生；第九的憍，依第五不敬尊師而生；第十的害，依止不忍而生；第十一的無慚與第十二的無愧，依第七毀增上戒而生；所剩餘的十二個隨煩惱就是從惛沈、掉舉、不信、懈怠、放逸、忘念、散亂、不正知、惡作、睡眠、尋、伺，依後二種毀增上心和毀增上慧而生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（連結：<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/C55-01.htm">隨煩惱依處、自性、毀三相門對照表</a>）</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、隨別廣2　玄一、釋差別2　黃一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨別廣，各別廣泛的解釋毀增上心及毀增上慧相應的隨煩惱，分二科；第一科釋差別，解釋差別相，又分二科；第一科標，標出毀增上心、毀增上慧由三門轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="75965:43410"></a>當知此中，毀增上心、毀增上慧由三門轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知毀增上心、毀增上慧，由三個處所有隨煩惱現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三門。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、由毀止相門，二、由毀舉相門，三、由毀捨相門。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由毀止相門：修止時有些隨煩惱會障礙修止。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、由毀舉相門：修舉時有些隨煩惱會障礙修舉。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、由毀捨相門：修捨時有些隨煩惱會障礙修捨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4432"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、明配屬</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明配屬，將止舉捨三門與隨煩惱配合起來解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">惛沈、睡眠，由初依處生；掉舉、惡作，由第二依處生；不信乃至尋伺，由第三依處生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　惛沈、睡眠出現時，對於所緣境心不明了，能破壞止相門。掉舉、惡作出現時，令心生雜染，能破壞舉相門。不信、懈怠、放逸、忘念、散亂、不正知、惡作、睡眠、尋、伺出現時，令心不平等，能破壞捨相門。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》惛沈睡眠由初依處生者：此說毀止相門，名初依處。毀舉相門，名第二依處。毀捨相門，名第三依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處說毀止相門名初依處。毀舉相門名第二依處。毀捨相門名第三依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、相應2　亥一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科相應，說明隨煩惱展轉相應的相狀，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，隨煩惱云何展轉相應？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，隨煩惱如何展轉相應？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋4　天一、與一切不善相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分四科；第一科與一切不善相應，說明中隨煩惱與一切不善相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知無慚、無愧，與一切不善相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知中隨煩惱的無慚、無愧，與一切不善相應。什麼是不善呢？據《大乘阿毘達磨集論》卷2〈1三法品〉說：「何等自性不善，謂除染污意相應及色無色界煩惱等，所餘能發惡行煩惱隨煩惱。」不善法的自性是指除了與第七識染污意相應的煩惱及色無色界煩惱等，所餘的就是欲界能引發惡行的根本煩惱及隨煩惱。當欲界眾生依第六意識造種種惡業時，一定有無慚及無愧心所相應，故說中隨煩惱無慚、無愧，與一切不善相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、與一切染汙心相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科與一切染汙心相應，說明不信等大隨煩惱與一切染污心相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不信、懈怠、放逸、忘念、散亂、惡慧，與一切染汙心相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不信、懈怠、放逸、忘念、散亂、惡慧等大隨煩惱，與一切染汙心相應。什麼是染汙心呢？據《大乘阿毘達磨集論》卷2〈1三法品〉說：「云何染污。謂不善及有覆無記法是染污義。有覆無記者，謂遍行意相應煩惱等，及色無色界繫諸煩惱等。」染汙心是指所有不善法現行時，與第七識染污意相應的煩惱，以及色無色界煩惱等。總之三界煩惱皆屬染污，與染污心相應的煩惱有不信、懈怠、放逸、忘念、散亂、惡慧等心所，故說不信、懈怠、放逸、忘念、散亂、惡慧，與一切染汙心相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、與一切善等相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科與一切善等相應，說明睡眠、惡作二種不定心所，與一切善、不善、無記相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4433"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">睡眠、惡作，與一切善、不善、無記相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　睡眠、惡作二種不定心所，遍與一切善、不善、無記等三性法相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天四、互不相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科互不相應，說明其他隨煩惱互不相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所餘當知互不相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其他隨煩惱如忿、恨、覆、惱、嫉、慳、誑、諂、憍、害等十種小隨煩惱，性質不同，不能俱時生起，而且是各別生起，故說不相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》所餘當知互不相應者：謂忿、恨、覆、惱、嫉、慳、誑、諂、憍、害十隨煩惱，展轉相違，故不俱起，名不相應。行相麤猛，各為主故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所餘是指忿、恨、覆、惱、嫉、慳、誑、諂、憍、害等十種小隨煩惱，性質不同，彼此展轉相違，不能俱時生起，名為不相應。這十種小隨煩惱行相比較麤顯強大，各有所主，各別生起，故說互不相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、世俗等2　亥一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科世俗等，分別隨煩惱的世俗有與實物有的差別相，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，隨煩惱幾世俗有？幾實物有？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，這麼多隨煩惱，哪一些屬於世俗有，是假有的？哪一些是屬於實物有，有自己的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂忿、恨、惱、嫉、害是瞋分故，皆世俗有；慳、憍、掉舉是貪分故，皆世俗有；覆、誑、諂、惛沈、睡眠、惡作是癡分故，皆世俗有；無慚、無愧、不信、懈怠是實物有；放逸是假有，如前說；忘念、散亂、惡慧是癡分故，一切皆是世俗有；尋、伺二種是發語言心加行分故，及慧分故，俱是假有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸隨煩惱中，忿、恨、惱、嫉、害是瞋的分位，都屬於世俗有；慳、憍、掉舉是貪的分位，也屬於世俗有；覆、誑、諂、惛沈、睡眠、惡作是癡的分位，也屬於世俗有；無慚、無愧、不信、懈怠有各別的體性，屬於實物有。放逸是假有，因為它以貪瞋癡及懈怠為體，不能精進的斷惡修善，是假有，如前文所說。忘念、散亂、惡慧是癡的分位，一切都是世俗有；尋伺二種是發語言心：思心所的加行分位，以及慧的分位，都是假有。〈攝事分〉卷100還會說到假有與實有的差別，此處是依據根本煩惱來說是假有。其實各別來說，諸隨煩惱都有各自的體性，由各自的種子而生的。此處是與根本煩惱對應來說的，因此有些論的安立與此略有不同。前文說不正知，此處說惡慧，其義相通，如《大乘百法明門論解》卷2所說：「不正知者，於所觀境謬解為性，能障正知，毀犯為業。毀犯業者，不正知者多毀犯故。此法或云慧一分攝，是煩惱相應慧故，《瑜伽》說此是癡分故。令知不正，名不正知。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》放逸是假有如前說者：前說不放逸，是無貪、無瞋、無癡、精進分故，即如是法治雜染義立不放逸。翻此當知放逸是世俗有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說不放逸，是無貪、無瞋、無癡、精進的分位，是這些法能對治雜染的道理，安立不放逸。相反的應當了知放逸是貪、瞋、癡、及懈怠的分位，是世俗有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、例前說2　戌一、軟品等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例前說，隨煩惱的軟中上品，例前根本煩惱所說可知，分二科；第一科軟品等，說明隨煩惱的軟中上品。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4434"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，隨煩惱云何成軟中上品？當知如本煩惱說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，隨煩惱如何成為軟中上品？應當了知如前根本煩惱所說可知。軟品，煩惱細微是最不容易斷，要以上品聖道來斷；中品就是中等的煩惱，以中品聖道來斷；上品是最粗的煩惱，最容易斷，以下品聖道最初所斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、事等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科事等，說明隨煩惱之事乃至所治，隨其所相應的，皆如根本煩惱所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是隨煩惱，若事、若差別、若過失、若所治，隨其所應，皆如煩惱應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是隨煩惱生起之所依事，十五種隨煩惱的差別，隨煩惱無有功德，有多過失，隨煩惱為十五種善法之所對治，隨煩惱或與根本煩惱相應，或是根本煩惱的分位差別，隨其所相應的，皆如前文根本煩惱處所說應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》隨其所應皆如煩惱應知者：前說煩惱依事而生，各有多別、有多過失，由善對治，成彼所治。如是諸隨煩惱與彼相應，或是彼分，隨其所應，如彼應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說根本煩惱依事而生，各有多種差別、有諸多過失，由善法對治，成善法之所對治。如是諸隨煩惱與根本煩惱相應，或是根本煩惱的分位差別，隨其所相應的根本煩惱種類，如前文所說應了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、無記性攝7　午一、依處2　未一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無記性攝，說明無記法的七種差別相，分七科；第一科依處，說明無記法的依止處，又分二科；第一科標，標出無記法的依止處有四種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，諸無記法依處，當知略有四種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，諸無記法的依止處，應當了知，要略而言有四種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，先出無記法的四種依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂業所引生；生已，若行住、若養命、若三摩地差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由業力引生的五蘊果報；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、五蘊生已，行住坐臥四威儀；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、養命之士農工商及各種技藝等工巧業處，</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、依三摩地，由無記心所發的神通變化等差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這四處所可以產生無記法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、自性2　未一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科自性，無記法的七種差別相，第二相說明無記法的自性，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，彼自性云何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，無記法的自性是怎麼樣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4435"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="52652:43450"></a>謂異熟生蘊，若中庸加行所攝威儀路及工巧處，若為嬉戲加行所攝變化。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無記法是指由業所引生的果報五蘊，無記心相應從事行住坐臥四威儀諸事；為活命從事士農工商、算數、計度，占象、咒術等工巧處；為了嬉戲，屬於無記心相應而作的神通變化。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷15：窺基大師說：據實義四種皆通三性，此處據總報為論，說異熟生蘊是無記，威儀路及工巧則以中庸加行簡非善惡性，變化以嬉戲簡非善性等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、相應2　未一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科相應，說明無記法展轉相應的相狀，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：彼云何展轉相應耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：無記法如何展轉相應呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、答2　申一、舉二種有2　酉一、標或有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科舉二種有，舉出二種無記法有時展轉相應，又分二科；第一科標或有，標出二種無記法或時展轉相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：威儀路、工巧處，或於一時展轉相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：只有行住坐臥等威儀路及士農工商等工巧處這二種無記法，有時候有展轉相應的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、舉經證</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科舉經證，舉經所說證明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如說或有事業，行時易作，非住、非坐、亦非偃臥；乃至或有事業，若行、若住、若坐、若臥皆悉易作。如經廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如經所說有些事業，行時容易作，比如比丘必須行往聚落乞食，非若住、若坐、及偃臥三種威儀；乃至有些事業，如攝心諸修行者，若行、若住、若坐、若臥，常應正念正知而住，熟修梵行者行住坐臥威儀都很容易攝心，如諸經有種種所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、簡所餘無</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡所餘無，簡別其餘無記法不能展轉相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所餘無有展轉相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其餘異熟生蘊，三摩地差別若為嬉戲加行所攝的變化，這二種無記法不能展轉相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、世俗等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科世俗等，無記法的七種差別相，第四相世俗等，說明無記法之世俗有與真實有的差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4436"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：是諸無記，幾實物有？幾是假有？答：於異熟所攝諸蘊及心加行差別中而施設故，當知一切皆世俗有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：諸無記法，有哪些是實物有？哪些是假有？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：無記法是依異熟（阿賴耶識）所攝五蘊施設異熟生蘊（前六轉識相應，雖酬業起非相續故，為有所簡名異熟生，即名世俗有）及心的活動不同，而施設威儀路、工巧處、及神通變化等，應當了知一切都屬世俗有，都是假有的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於異熟所攝諸蘊等者：依異熟所攝諸蘊，是故施設異熟生蘊。依心加行差別，施設威儀路、工巧處及與變化。故彼一切皆世俗有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於異熟所攝的五蘊，假名施設異熟生蘊，是世俗有。依止心的加行不同，就有威儀路、工巧處、及神通變化等行為出現，故一切無記法都是世俗有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午五、軟品等3　未一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科軟品等，無記法的七種差別相，第五相軟品等，說明無記法的軟中上品差別，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何彼成軟中上品？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸無記法怎麼樣成為軟中上品？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋2　申一、約相對辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科約相對辨，約相對來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂異熟生及威儀路不猛利故，俱是軟品；諸工巧處性猛利故，說名中品；當知變化性極猛利，故是上品。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　異熟生的五蘊，還有行住坐臥等威儀路，任運而作，性質不猛利，都屬於軟品。士農工商等工巧處，需要用心作，性質比較猛利，屬於中品。神通變化要有強大的定力，心的性質非常猛利，是屬於上品。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、約各別辨2　酉一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約各別辨，說明無記法各別的相狀，分二科；第一科標，標出無記法各有差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又四種類，各有差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又四種無記法各有各的差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋4　戌一、異熟三品</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分四科；第一科異熟三品，說明異熟三品差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂無色界異熟是軟品，色界異熟是中品，欲界異熟是上品。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無色界的果報是很微細，只有心，沒有色，屬於軟品。色界的果報有色有心，行相比無色界的果報粗一點，屬於中品。欲界的果報，身心都很粗重，屬於上品。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4437"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、威儀三品</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科威儀三品，說明威儀路三品差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若坐、若臥是軟威儀，住是中威儀，行是上威儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　坐著跟躺著屬於軟品的威儀，住是中品的威儀，走路行相最粗，屬於上品威儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、工巧三品</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科工巧三品，說明工巧處三品差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初習業者是下工巧，已串習者是中工巧，堪為師者是上工巧。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　工巧處中，初修習者還不熟練，屬於下品工巧；已經串習一段時間，屬於中品工巧；已經熟練善巧能夠當老師指導他人的，屬於上品工巧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、變化三品</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科變化三品，說明神通變化三品差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">下品修三摩地所得是軟變化，中品修三摩地所得是中變化，上品修三摩地所得是上變化。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依下品的定力所得的神通屬於軟品；依中品的定力所得的神通屬於中品；依上品的定力所得的神通屬於上品。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等類，軟中上品差別應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說四種無記法，隨不同情況各有軟中上品差別，應當要了解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午六、依事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科依事，無記法的七種差別相，第六相依事，說明無記法生的依止事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：是諸無記依何事生？答：當知略說依十二事。如聞所成地已說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：這些無記依止何種事情而生呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：應當了知，要略而言依十二事而生，如〈聞所成地〉已經說過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4438"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如聞所成地已說者：聞所成地說有十二工巧業處。謂營農工業、商賈工業、事王工業、書算計度數印工業、占相工業、呪術工業、營造工業、生成工業、防邪工業、和合工業、成熟工業、音樂工業。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/15.htm#43484:13255">陵本十五卷二十二頁1360</a>）由是當知，此中問答，唯約工巧為論，非餘一切。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈聞所成地〉卷15，570頁說有十二種工巧業處，包括營農工業：事農、商賈工業、事王工業：在政府部門作事、書算計度數印工業：文書、代書、會計、印刷等、占相工業：算命及看風水地理等事、呪術工業：持明咒等、營造工業：建築方面之事、生成工業：畜養六畜等事、防邪工業：指織繡等事，中國人多以女工從事，龜茲及印度人多以男工從事，翻譯時保存本音以男聲呼之，所以名為防邪、和合工業：能調解鬥訟等事、成熟工業：指燒飯做菜成熟飲食等事、音樂工業：音樂歌舞等事。由此應當了知，此文中之問答，唯約工巧無記為論，不是指其它異熟無記、威儀無記、及變化無記。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午七、差別2　未一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科差別，無記法的七種差別相，最後一相差別，說明無記法的差別，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="40835:43486"></a>云何諸無記差別？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些無記法有什麼差別？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋2　申一、別辨4　酉一、異熟生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科別辨，各別說明，又分四科；第一科異熟生，說明異熟生五蘊的五種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂異熟生，五趣別故，五種差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　異熟生的五蘊有五趣的差別；有天、人、地獄、餓鬼、畜生等五趣，故有五種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、威儀路</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科威儀路，說明威儀路有四種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若威儀路，威儀別故，四種差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　威儀路只有行住坐臥四種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、工巧處</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科工巧處，說明工巧處有十二種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若工巧處，十二事差別故，即十二種差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　工巧處如前所說有營農等十二種事，就有十二種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、變化心2　戌一、舉八種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科變化心，說明變化心有八種差別，分二科；第一科舉八種，舉出神通有八種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">異生、聲聞、獨覺、菩薩、如來差別故，為嬉戲、為利他、身語變化差別故，當知變化八種差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以能現神通者有凡夫、聲聞、獨覺、菩薩、如來等五種差別，由現神通之動機有為嬉戲或為利他差別二種差別，再加上現神通之身語變化差別，應當了知變化有八種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4439"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、顯攝餘</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯攝餘，顯示如上所說八種變化即含攝其餘變化狀況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此差別即攝餘事，故不別說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由此八種變化差別，就包括餘變化事，故不再各別說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》當知變化八種差別者：補特伽羅差別有五，謂異生、聲聞、獨覺、菩薩，及與如來。所為差別有二，謂為嬉戲，或為利他。所變化事差別有二，謂身及語。如是變化，總有八種差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>
