<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》是四顛倒所依處故者：常、樂、淨、我名四顛倒應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知對常、樂、淨、我的執著，名為四顛倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、斷集</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科斷集，說明應斷集。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">雖遍知苦，仍為集諦之所隨逐，故須更說永斷集諦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　雖然徧知苦諦，可是仍然還是被集諦的煩惱種子及業種子所隨逐，必須斷除集諦才能離苦，因此必須再說永斷集諦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4454"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、證滅</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科證滅，證得滅諦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">言觸證者，是現見義。由於滅諦現前見故，不生怖畏，愛樂攝受，是故次說觸證滅諦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說觸證是指現量證得諸法實相，名現見義，又名現觀。由於現量證得諸法實相，對於寂滅的境界不生怖畏，也愛樂攝受滅諦涅槃安樂的功德，所以其次說觸證滅諦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不生怖畏愛樂攝受者：已見諦者，離我顛倒，證知我我定非有故，是故於寂靜界不生怖畏，深心欣仰愛樂攝受故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　已經見得四諦真實相的人，不會再有常、樂、淨、我的四顛倒，現量證知五蘊決定無我無我所，這樣入寂靜的境界，於一切相不現時，不生怖畏，甚至感覺身心脫落，如釋重負，深深地欣仰愛樂攝受這種寂靜的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、修道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科修道，說明應勤修道乃能成辦所說三義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若勤修道，乃能成辦所說三義，是故後說修習道諦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要很精進修習聖道，才能成辦徧知苦諦、斷除集諦、觸證滅諦的三種功德，因此最後說修習道諦，要有正確的方法才能達到目的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅六、辨諦現觀2　卯一、總2　辰一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科辨諦現觀，辨明諦現觀，現觀又名知法、現法、入法、正見、正觀、如實知等，是指以無漏慧，親切、清晰地覺知四聖諦，分二科；第一科總，總相說明現觀的種類及定義，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：諦現觀有幾種？此復何相？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：諦現觀有哪些種類？其中有什麼相貌？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、答2　巳一、明體相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明相應，說明現觀相應時的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="8163:43675"></a>答：決定義是現觀義。此則於諸諦中決定智慧及彼因、彼相應、彼共有法為體，是名現觀相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　窺基大師解釋此文說，於四聖諦有決定的智慧，名現觀；包括信現觀、思現觀、戒現觀、現觀智諦現觀、現觀邊智諦現觀、究竟現觀等六種現觀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：對四聖諦的道理產生決定不變的無漏智慧，是現觀義。對於四聖諦生起的決定智慧，是指現觀智諦現觀、現觀邊智諦現觀、究竟現觀三種；及生起現觀的因是指思現觀，思現觀是在加行位所生起的，加行位時，要一直不斷的思惟觀察諸法的真實相，此時與喜相應，有思現觀以後，才能夠成就現觀智諦現觀的根本智，現觀邊智諦現觀的後得智，乃至究竟現觀的無學智；彼相應是指信現觀，行者證入現觀時，一定會對三寶及戒有深刻的信心名四證信；彼共有法是指戒現觀，行者證入現觀時，無漏的戒法也會現前。以上面所說的六種現觀為體，稱為現觀相。《顯揚聖教論》卷16〈8成現觀品〉說：入現觀前，先從聞所生智乃至世間第一法智等世間有漏智，思惟簡擇四諦的道理到究竟圓滿，且對於所觀察諸諦境中，不由加行功用，任運決定生起相，名現觀相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於諸諦中決定智慧等者：此中智慧，通說加行、根本、後得三無漏慧。聞思修三能成彼慧，是名彼因。彼助伴法，名彼相應。彼所依緣，名共有法。總此一切，為現觀體。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於諸諦中決定智慧這一段文中的智慧，通說加行無分別智、根本無分別智、後得無分別智三種無漏慧。依聞思修三法能成就這三種無漏慧，是達到現觀的原因，名為彼因。彼助伴法是與現觀相應的心所法，稱為彼相應。入現觀時，所依止的意根，所緣的真如境，名共有法，總合這一切因緣，為現觀的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4455"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、出種類</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出種類，說出現觀的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復六種應知，如有尋有伺地說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知現觀共有六種，如前〈有尋有伺地〉所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此復六種等者：謂思現觀、信現觀、戒現觀、現觀智諦現觀、現觀邊智諦現觀、究竟現觀。如有尋有伺地說應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/10.htm#43681:8157">陵本十卷十九頁832</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現觀共有六種；思現觀、信現觀、戒現觀、現觀智諦現觀、現觀邊智諦現觀、究竟現觀。如〈有尋有伺等三地〉卷10，345頁所說，應當了知。也可參考〈決擇‧聲聞地〉卷71，2198頁，二十二種現觀差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、別5　辰一、思現觀</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別，各別說明六現觀的體性，分五科；第一科思現觀，說明於諸諦決定思惟名思現觀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中云何名初現觀？謂於諸諦決定思惟。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六現觀中第一個思現觀是什麼意思？是指對於四諦的道理，有決定性的思惟，名思現觀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《顯揚聖教論》卷17〈8成現觀品〉說：若有成就思現觀的人，能正確了知諸行無常、諸受皆苦、諸法無我、涅槃寂靜，雖然還是凡夫，已能如是決定解了一切，沙門、婆羅門、諸天魔梵及餘世間人，決定不能引奪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、信現觀</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科信現觀，說明信現觀通於凡聖，於三寶所三種淨信，由於寶義已決定故，及聞所成決定智慧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為第二現觀？謂三寶所三種淨信，由於寶義已決定故，及聞所成決定智慧。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二信現觀是什麼意思？是指對於佛法僧三寶有三種淨信，對於所謂的寶義，已經決定真實是寶，屬於聖人無漏的淨信；及聞所成決定智慧，屬於凡位有漏的淨信。《顯揚聖教論》卷17〈8成現觀品〉說：若有成就信現觀的人，或住異生位或住聖位，於現生或於現生來生終不宣說，於異眾中別有佛，別有善說法，別有正行僧。無論凡聖都相信唯佛法僧是真實三寶，於其他宗教或眾生中再無三寶可得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、戒現觀</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科戒現觀，說明於惡趣業，已得決定不作律儀名戒現觀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為第三現觀？謂聖所愛戒，於惡趣業已得決定不作律儀故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三戒現觀是什麼意思？是指聖所愛戒，聖人身善口善意善，不造惡業，都是喜歡持戒清淨的，因為有別解脫戒、定共戒也成就道共戒，決定不會故意造作到三惡道的十不善業，對於三惡道已經成就「非擇滅」的功德，名戒現觀。《顯揚聖教論》卷17〈8成現觀品〉說：若有成就戒現觀的人，乃至畜生終不故害其命，及不與取，行邪淫行，知而妄語、飲窣羅迷隷耶末陀放逸處酒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、現觀智及現觀邊智諦現觀2　巳一、廣分別2　午一、現觀智諦現觀2　未一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科現觀智及現觀邊智諦現觀，說明現觀智及現觀邊智諦現觀，分二科；第一科廣分別，詳細分別這二種現觀，又分二科；第一科現觀智諦現觀，說現觀智諦現觀。現觀智指於諦現前觀察的智慧，現觀邊智是證入現觀智以後生起的通於世間及出世間的後得智。這二個合起來解釋，會有很多學問了，可以參考其他經論所說，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4456"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為第四現觀？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四現觀智諦現觀是什麼意思？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋2　申一、辨相2　酉一、初現觀位3　戌一、三心差別3　亥一、內遣有情假</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科辨相，說明現觀智諦現觀的相狀，現觀智諦現觀屬於見道位，包括二種現觀；初現觀位及第二現觀位，即是所謂的真見道及相見道，又分二科；第一科初現觀位，說明初現觀位，初現觀是所謂的真見道，三心真見道，又分三科；第一科三心差別，說明三心差別，緣我空、法空、我法二空真如，名三心差別，又分三科；第一科內遣有情假，真見道證唯識性與根本無分別智相應：識不可得，識所現的相也不可得，證得法性；相見道證唯識相：帶相緣如與後得智相應，緣真如相，有見有相，證得法相，初現觀位內心遣除我相假安立法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　請參考連結檔（連結：<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/C55-02.htm">真見道與相見道</a>）</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂於加行道中，先集資糧極圓滿故，又善方便磨瑩心故，從世間順決擇分邊際善根無間，有初內遣有情假法緣心生，能除軟品見道所斷煩惱麤重。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　初現觀位是指在煖、頂、忍、世第一加行位修學聖道時，過去順解脫分位積聚的六波羅蜜等修道資糧已經圓滿了；又能善巧琢磨這一念心，令其清淨光明；從世間順決擇分邊際世第一法一剎那入見道位時，有三心生起來，名三心真見道。最剛開始的這一念心，遣除緣假相安立的有情想，就是遣除我執，證得我空真如，生起無分別智名法緣心生，能斷除軟品指最粗的見道所斷之煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》有初內遣有情假法緣心生者：諸有情名唯假相有，無始時來熏習執著，是名有情假法。入現觀時，除遣彼相正智得生，名初內遣有情假法緣心生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸多有情的名字只是假相有法而已，無始劫來眾生熏習執著認為五蘊是我，名有情假法。證入現觀時，除遣有情假法之我相，與我空真如相應的無分別智現前，名為初內遣有情假法緣心生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、內遣諸法假</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科內遣諸法假，證入現觀的第二念心能斷法執。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">從此無間，第二內遣諸法假法緣心生，能除中品見道所斷煩惱麤重。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從此沒有間斷的，第二念心除遣法執，通達一切法唯假名安立，是不真實的，生起的無分別智，能夠除掉中品的見道所斷的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》第二內遣諸法假法緣心生者：諸法名義唯假安立，是言所行，不稱實有，是名諸法假法。入現觀時，除遣彼相正智得生，是名第二內遣諸法假法緣心生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸法的名字及名所詮的境界，只是假名安立，是語言所活動的地方，不是真實有，名為諸法假法。如說桌子，言說中並沒有真實的桌子存在，桌子即非桌子，是名桌子，不但桌子的名字是假安立，連桌子所詮的境界也無真實體性可得。證入現觀時，除遣諸法假法之法我相，與法空真如相應的無分別智現前，名為第二內遣諸法假法緣心生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、遍遣一切有情諸法假</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科遍遣一切有情諸法假，證入現觀的第三念心能斷我法二執。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">從此無間，第三遍遣一切有情諸法假法緣心生，能除一切見道所斷煩惱麤重。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從此沒有間斷的，第三念心完全除遣對於假名安立的一切有情及諸法的執著，與我法二空真如相應的無分別智現前，能夠斷除一切見道所斷最微細的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4457"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、止觀雙運2　亥一、標名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科止觀雙運，說明止觀雙運的相狀，分二科；第一科標名，標出止觀雙運的名字。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此現觀即是見道，亦名雙運道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又此三心現觀，就是見道，又名雙運道，止觀雙運。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋由</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋由，解釋止觀雙運。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中雖有毗鉢舍那品三心及奢摩他品三心，然由雙運合立三心，以於一剎那中止觀俱可得故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這三心，如前文說，起一心其實有眾多心，說一心見道，或三心見道，其實都經過很多剎那，不是說一剎那即完成這件事，由多剎那相似，說為起一心。現觀時雖然毗鉢舍那的觀有三品心，一是我空觀，二是法空觀，三是我法二空觀；及奢摩他的止品也有三心，然而現觀時止觀雙運合起來安立三心，不說有六心，因為現觀時於每一剎那中都同時有止又有觀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、緣境相應2　亥一、緣境</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科緣境相應，說明現觀三心緣境相應情形，分二科；第一科緣境，說明現觀緣非安立諦境。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此諸心，唯緣非安立諦境。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知現觀時三心，唯以離名言相的真如為所緣境，此時言語道斷、心行處滅，因為沒有名字，心裡不能動，是無分別的境界，名緣非安立諦境。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科相應，說明三心相應的智慧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又前二心，法智相應；第三心，類智相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又前二心與我空真如、法空真如相應的無分別智名法智相應；第三心與二空真如相應的無分別智名類智相應。《雜集論》卷9說見道三心都是法智，因為同觀諸法真如，此處所說類智，指第三心與前面二心同一種類，名為類智。《成唯識論》卷9說：一觀非安立諦有三品心。一、內遣有情假緣智，能除軟品分別隨眠。二、內遣諸法假緣智，能除中品分別隨眠。三、遍遣一切有情諸法假緣智，能除一切分別隨眠。前二名法智，各別緣故，第三名類智，總合（我法二空）緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又前二心法智相應等者：於內共了、現見所知諸義境界無漏之智，是名法智。於不共了、不現見所知義境無漏之智，是名類智。義如顯揚論說。（二卷十六頁）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者緣欲界四諦修習止觀，證入現觀時，通達欲界現見五蘊有情假及法假，生我空智及法空智的無漏智慧，名為法智。緣色、無色界四諦，通達上二界不現見五蘊、四蘊有情假及法假，證得的無漏智慧，名為類智。《瑜伽論記》說三心見道是指菩薩說的，因為聲聞不修法空智。我法二空智，應該是屬於菩薩。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4458"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、第二現觀位</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二現觀位，現觀智諦現觀有二個現觀位，第一個現觀位有三念心，第二個現觀位，因為緣安立諦相，又稱為十六心相見道，也是屬於見道位的現觀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又即由此心勢力故，於苦等安立諦中，有第二現觀位清淨無礙苦等智生；</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於此真見道無分別智的勢力，於名言安立的四諦當中，有第二現觀位的相見道，那時帶相緣如，清淨沒有障礙的，不屬於戲論而起的，沒有煩惱隨眠在裡面的苦集滅道四諦的後得智慧現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》有第二現觀位等者：緣非安立諦境，於現觀位說名為初。此言安立諦境，從彼無間所生，是故名第二現觀位。於此位中，彼苦等智，於安立諦能善通達真如性故，不為煩惱所隨眠故，非依名言戲論起故，是名清淨無礙。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　緣離名言相的真如為所緣境，名為初現觀位。此處說安立諦境，安立諦指名言安立的四諦，緣安立諦境，是帶相緣如。以唯識而言，即是證得唯識相，從初現觀位後無間所生後得智，是第二個現觀位。於第二現觀位中，依苦集滅道的智慧，能通達名言安立苦集滅道四諦的真如理，心裡沒有煩惱種子的障礙，由於依無分別智力量的餘勢來觀察四諦的真如理，故此後得智也不是名言戲論所生，說名清淨無礙。應當了知依此後得智，相見道時，苦集滅道四聖諦的智慧就能夠成立了。第二現觀位是成立苦集滅道四智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知依此智故，苦集滅道智得成立。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知依此後得智而通達名言安立的苦集滅道四諦之真實義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、出體</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出體，說明現觀智諦現觀的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即前三心并止觀品，能證見斷煩惱寂滅，能得永滅一切煩惱及所依事出世間道，是名現觀智諦現觀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　即前初現觀三心及止觀雙運三品，能證得見道所斷的煩惱寂滅，修道位時以此出世間聖道，能夠永遠滅除一切煩惱的種子，以及生死所依的五蘊，不再到三界五趣受生，成就究竟現觀，名為現觀智諦現觀。由初見道力，展轉能引金剛喻定最後學道永滅修惑，修惑斷盡，將來果報不生，成就無學究竟現觀，都要依止現觀智諦現觀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《成唯識論》卷9說：「現觀智諦現觀，是指一切種緣非安立根本、後得無分別智。」現觀，指現前之觀境，一切種者即真如，以真如與一切法為體故，以真如名一切種；智，是指能觀之智；諦，指非安立諦，此無漏智現觀緣非安立諦故名現觀智諦現觀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《成唯識論》卷9說：見道略說有二種，包括一、真見道，二、相見道。其中真見道有二種說法，一種主張二空二障漸證漸斷，所以三心真見道，如此處所說，及〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷59，1953所說；一種主張二空二障頓證頓斷，所以一心真見道，如〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷58，1936所說。《成唯識論》較偏重於一心真見道說，因此將三心見道安立為相見道，說相見道有三心相見道及十六心相見道。本論此處主張三心真見道，十六心相見道，可看出現觀智諦現觀，包括緣真如為境的根本、後得二種無分別智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》永滅一切煩惱及所依事者：三界見、修所斷煩惱皆悉永斷，是名永滅一切煩惱。當來後有眾苦皆悉永斷，是名滅所依事。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三界見、修所斷的煩惱全部斷除，名為永滅一切煩惱。將來輪轉生死的五蘊也全部斷除，不再領受生死苦果，名為滅所依事。現觀智諦現觀就是證得無分別智，依止現觀智諦現觀可以成就究竟現觀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、現觀邊智諦現觀2　未一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科現觀邊智諦現觀，說明現觀邊智諦現觀的體相，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為現觀邊智諦現觀？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是現觀邊智諦現觀？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋2　申一、辨相5　酉一、出智體</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科辨相，說明現觀邊智諦現觀的相狀，又分五科；第一科出智體，現觀邊智諦現觀的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4459"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂此現觀後所得智，名現觀邊智。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　初現觀後所得的是現觀邊智，也名為後得智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、明智依</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明智依，說明現觀邊智依止什麼心生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此智，第三心無間，從見道起方現在前。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知現觀邊智是依初現觀位的第三心之後，無間生起現觀邊智，從見道位後才現前成就的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、顯緣境</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科顯緣境，說明現觀邊智諦現觀的所緣境。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">緣先世智曾所觀察下上二地及二增上安立諦境。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現觀邊智是緣以前加行位時，帶有名言相的四諦世智名先世智，就是依著教法所認識的四諦的智慧，曾經所觀察的下上二地，即欲界、色界及無色界的苦集二諦，及滅道二諦為所緣境。二增上安立諦，增上指滅諦及道諦能趣向解脫，所以名增上。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、辨所攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科辨所攝，分別現觀邊智諦現觀所攝智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">似法、類智，世俗智攝，通世出世，是出世間智後所得。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現觀邊智，相似但不同於現觀位的法智與類智，屬世俗智攝。由於有名言相，帶相緣如，因此屬於世間；又由於沒有煩惱種子，也不是由名言戲論所生，因此又屬於出世間，所以現觀邊智是通於世出世間的，是得出世間智以後所得到的智慧，稱為現觀邊智，也名後得智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》緣先世智曾所觀察等者：先加行位，以世間智，觀察欲、色、無色苦集二諦，是名觀察下上二地安立諦境。又復觀察彼苦集滅及能滅道，名觀察二增上安立諦境。今此位中，於彼安立得如實知，然不應說法智、類智所攝，以彼唯緣非安立諦境生故。今此不爾，緣安立諦下上地別，是故說言似法、類智，世俗智攝。非唯世間，非唯出世，是故說言通世出世，是出世間智後所得。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　先加行位以世間智，依名言安立的佛法所得的智慧，觀察下地欲界、上地色界和無色界的苦集二諦，名為觀察下上二地安立諦境。又觀察下上二地苦集寂滅的滅諦及能滅的道諦，名為觀察二增上安立諦境。在後得智的階段，對於名言安立的四聖諦能夠如實的了知，可是他不是真見道，屬於相見道，不能說是法智、類智所攝，因為法智和類智，唯緣離言的非安立諦境而生。而後得智是不一樣的，後得智是緣著安立諦的下上二地之四諦差別而生，是相似於法智、類智，屬於世俗智攝。此現觀邊智不是只是世間的智慧，因為此智生時沒有煩惱種子隨逐，又非名言戲論所生；也不能說完全是出世間的智慧，因為緣安立諦，故說通世出世，是成就出世間根本無分別智以後所得到的智慧，又名後得智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉五、釋差別2　戌一、約所取能取辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科釋差別，解釋後得智的差別相，分二科；第一科約所取能取辨，由所取、能取來說明後得智的差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4460"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如其次第，於一一諦二種智生，謂忍可欲樂智，及現觀決定智。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如所觀四諦的次第，在每一諦中有二種智慧產生，第一種名忍可欲樂智，是認可、承認、歡喜，好樂四諦道理的智慧；第二種名現觀決定智，是現前現量觀察四諦，於四諦道理生起決定不移的智慧，通達苦真實是苦，乃至道真實是道的真實義。忍與智有什麼差別呢？修行時，有無間道、有解脫道，忍是斷煩惱時，屬於無間道，智是證理時，屬於解脫道，忍的下一剎就是智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、約下上諦境辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約下上諦境辨，以三界四諦的所緣境界，來說明後得智的差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是依前現觀起已，於下上諸諦中，二二智生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是依止前面的現觀生起以後，於下欲界、上色無色界苦集滅道四諦的行相，每一個諦都有忍可欲樂智，及有現觀決定智這二種智慧產生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、結名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結名，結語名稱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名現觀邊智諦現觀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總合起來，名為現觀邊智諦現觀，是後得智所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於下上諸諦中二二智生者：謂於下上二地一一諦中，各復有其二智生故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於下欲界、上色無色界的三界四諦中，每一諦中，各有忍可欲樂智及現觀決定智這二種智慧產生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、總料簡2　午一、辨差別3　未一、無有分別異</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科總料簡，廣分別了現觀智及現觀邊智諦現觀後，現在總料簡這一科，將現觀智諦現觀、還有現觀邊智諦現觀，再合在一起，思量簡別一番，分二科；第一科辨差別，說明現觀智諦現觀與現觀邊智諦現觀的差別，又分三科；第一科無有分別異，說明第一種差別，現觀智諦現觀是無分別的，現觀邊智諦現觀是有分別的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中前智遣假法緣故，是無分別；後智隨逐假法緣故，是有分別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此中前面的現觀智諦現觀所成就的根本無分別智，是遣除有情假、法假及雙遣二假為緣所生，是無分別的；後面的現觀邊智諦現觀所成就的後得智，因為隨逐聖教安立的四諦觀察假法為緣所生，是有分別的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、能斷不生異</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科能斷不生異，第二種差別，現觀智諦現觀能斷煩惱，現觀邊智諦現觀令所斷的煩惱不生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又前智於依止中，能斷見斷煩惱隨眠；後智思惟所緣故，令彼所斷更不復起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又前現觀智諦現觀所成就的根本無分別智，於依止的五蘊中，能夠斷除見道所斷的煩惱種子；而現觀邊智諦現觀所成就的後得智，能思惟所緣四諦的道理，令無分別智所斷除的煩惱不再現起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》後智思惟所緣故者：思惟安立諸諦為所緣故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為後得智思惟名言安立的四聖諦為所緣，使令斷除的煩惱不會再生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4461"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、進趣斷道異</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科進趣斷道異，第三種差別，前根本無分別智能進趣修道中的出世斷道，後得智能進趣修道中的世出世斷道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又前智能進趣修道中出世斷道，第二智能進趣世出世斷道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又前現觀智諦現觀成就的根本無分別智，能夠在修道位中，成就出世聖道斷除修道位所要斷的煩惱種子，屬於出世斷道；現觀邊智諦現觀成就的後得智，能夠在修道位中，使所斷的煩惱種子不再生起，因為緣於名言相，是屬於世出世斷道。二種智慧功能不同，現觀智諦現觀能斷煩惱，現觀邊智諦現觀能隨順引發現觀智諦現觀，是配合著一直往前進，直到究竟現觀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、簡方便3　未一、標非</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡方便，簡別這二種方法各有功能，缺一不可，分三科；第一科標非，說明單世間智不能斷除煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無有純世間道能永害隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一般禪定或在加行位時，都屬於純世間道，只是緣名言安立的四諦，不能斷除煩惱的種子。《瑜伽論記》景法師說：這段文是為了簡別二乘認為後得智一向有漏是純世間。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋由2　申一、出相引</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋由，解釋純世間道不能斷除煩惱種子的理由，分二科；第一科出相引，說明純世間道有相執，所以不能斷除煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由世間道是曾習故，相執所引故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於世間道的修行帶名言相，是過去曾經修習過的，都還是在名言相當中不斷的熏習，有名言就有相，是相執所引發的，有相就會有執著，故世間道不能斷除煩惱的種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、顯無能</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯無能，顯示有相執不能斷除煩惱種子的原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如相執所引，如是亦不能泯伏諸相；如不能泯伏諸相，如是亦不能永害麤重。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　雖然行者緣四諦法相，由於有相就有執著，以相不能除相，無力滅除種種法相，必須離相才能夠除相，故不能永斷煩惱種子。《瑜伽論記》中景法師說，因為後得智是：一、緣名言安立的四諦。二、是曾習故。三、是相執所引。不能泯伏三界法相，由此後得智有這三種條件，故不能斷除煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、結成</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結成，結說成有相執的純世間道不能斷除煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故彼道無有永害諸隨眠義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　世間道的世間定或加行位有漏的修道，還是有名言相的執著，所以不能斷除煩惱的種子。〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷33開始處，1063頁也曾提到，成就未到地定以上的人，有二種道路可以走，一種是世間道，一種是出世間道。世間道就是朝向禪定的，初禪、二禪、三禪、四禪。出世間道是修四聖諦，苦集滅道四聖諦，唯出世間道才能夠斷除煩惱種子。世間道在禪定中，不論禪定多高，還是有名言相在其中，故不能斷除煩惱的種子；有漏的修道還帶名言，也不能斷除煩惱種子，要斷除煩惱的種子，必須離名言相，遠離分別，得無分別智才能斷除煩惱。故說無有純世間道能斷除煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》相執所引故者：謂世間道非自內證，唯從他聞，不離名言戲論相執，名彼所引。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　世間道不是自己親身體證的，只是從老師那裡聽到，不能遠離名言戲論相執，名為彼所引，想要以名相去除名相是不能的，有相執時，不能泯伏諸相，所以世間道不能永害煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從無有純世間道能永害隨眠到是故彼道無有永害諸隨眠義，據《瑜伽論記》卷15有幾種不同解釋，筆者略譯如下：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、景法師解釋此文：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 這一大段文是為了簡別二乘認為後得智一向有漏是純世間。又解釋為何後得智不是純世間道中，說是曾習故者，指修道中之後得智是相見道所顯，名為曾習。而世間修道唯是有漏，不名後得智故。今所執修道後得智通世出世二種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 相執引故者，相執即是末那二執。入真現觀時(真見道時)二執不起，現在出真現觀時相執還起。引出彼後得智由有三相：（1）緣名言安立的四諦，（2）是曾習故，（3）是相執所引，不能泯伏三界法相。由此三義不能永害隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、神泰法師解釋此文：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 這一大段文是為了簡別後得智不能斷煩惱的原因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 因為後得智緣事故名純世間道，不約無漏義名出世間。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 是曾習故者，無分別智後才得此後得智，因此名曾習。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4. 又此緣事之無相無分別智之後得智是曾習，與有漏種類之世間道同故，如有漏心相執之所引，所以遂令後得智也有相，乃至廣說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　5. 又解，純世間道是有漏智無能斷煩惱。若是如此，為何置於此文，有何意義？答：此中但簡後得智不能斷惑的原因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　關於後得智能否斷煩惱種子，依《成唯識論》卷10有二種說法：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 有義根本無分別智親證二空所顯真理，無境相故能斷隨眠，後得不然故非斷道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 有義後得無分別智雖不親證二空真理無力能斷迷理隨眠，而於安立非安立相明了現前無倒證故亦能永斷迷事隨眠。故《瑜伽論記》說修道位中有出世斷道世出世斷道，無純世間道能永害隨眠，是曾習故、相執引故。由斯理趣諸見所斷及修所斷迷理隨眠唯有根本無分別智親證理故能正斷彼，餘修所斷迷事隨眠根本後得俱能正斷。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　窺基大師於《成唯識論掌中樞要》卷2解釋這段文說：前師釋修道中世出世斷道者，此依菩薩修道有獨用無分別智，名世出世道，有真俗合用智斷。如舉勝者，下下地者斷障雖不由俗然必俱時，若不爾者，豈後勝地要唯無分別智，不與後得俱方斷惑耶。初唯出世斷通三乘，後兼菩薩故作是說。二理教齊，任情取捨。窺基大師意指若說唯根本無分別智能斷煩惱種子，這是通於三乘所說，若說後得無分別智能斷見道後修所斷迷事隨眠，是在二乘非菩薩位，因為菩薩因中不斷煩惱迷事惑故。這二種說法都有教證可得，任君取捨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文的解釋，《瑜伽論記》卷15與窺基大師於《成唯識論掌中樞要》卷2解釋有很大不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、究竟現觀2　巳一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科究竟現觀，說明究竟現觀的體相，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4462"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為究竟現觀？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是作究竟現觀？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋3　午一、出智別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科出智別，說明究竟現觀有二種智慧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂由永斷修所斷故，所有盡智、無生智生。或一向出世，或通世出世。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　究竟現觀時，由於永斷修道所斷的煩惱種子，成就煩惱斷盡的盡智及苦果不生的無生智。這二種智慧或一向出世間，屬於勝義諦所攝的根本無分別智；或通於世出世間，屬於世俗諦所攝的後得智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、釋得名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋得名，解釋究竟現觀的名字。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於現法中，一切煩惱永斷決定故；於當來世，一切依事永滅決定故；名究竟現觀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在現在的色受想行識當中，一切煩惱永遠斷除，決定不再生起任何愛見煩惱，成就盡智；於來生一切依事是三界五趣的果報永遠滅除，決定不再受生，成就無生智；得到這二種智慧，名為究竟現觀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》盡智無生智者：謂阿羅漢於諸煩惱究竟盡中，發起盡智。由因盡故，當來苦果畢竟不生，即於此中起無生智。義如聲聞地說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/34.htm#43764:28188">陵本三十四卷二十四頁2807</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　阿羅漢於究竟斷盡三界愛見煩惱，發起盡智。因為三界的愛見煩惱斷除，招感苦果的因斷了，將來不會再有一個果報體現前，成就無生智。道理如〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷34，1117頁所說應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、辨差別2　未一、盡智攝2　申一、一向出世</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科辨差別，說明盡智和無生智的差別，分二科；第一科盡智攝，說明盡智所攝的二類智慧，又分二科；第一科一向出世，說明一向出世，屬於勝義諦所攝的盡智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等名為出世盡智？謂若智，於盡無分別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是出世間的盡智？是指於斷盡煩惱，真實成就無分別智，遠離能所、語言、根、塵、識、器世間的虛妄分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、通世出世</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科通世出世，說明通世出世，屬於世俗諦所攝的盡智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等名為世出世盡智？謂若智，於盡有分別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼稱作世出世間的盡智？盡智在後得智的階段，帶有名言分別時，能令所斷煩惱不起，名通世、出世間，是屬於世俗諦所攝的盡智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4463"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、無生智攝2　申一、一向出世</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無生智攝，說明無生智所攝的二類智慧，分二科；第一科一向出世，說明一向出世，屬於勝義諦所攝的無生智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等名為出世無生智？謂即此依事滅因義故，於當來世依事不生中所有無分別智。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼稱作出世間的無生智？是在生起所依的果報事之煩惱因完全滅除時，於當來世五蘊不生中所成就的無分別智，名為出世的無生智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、通世出世</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科通世出世，說明通世出世，屬於世俗諦所攝的無生智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等名為世出世無生智？謂於當來世依事不生中所有有分別智。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼稱作世出世間的無生智？是出世的無生智下一剎那生起的後得智，於當來世五蘊不生中所成就的有分別智，名為通於世出世的無生智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、約三諦辨2　寅一、斥他3　卯一、略標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約三諦辨，分二科；第一科斥他，訶斥外道的錯誤執著。這段文主要為破邪顯正，因為《阿含經》上說，出家梵志，應該有三種婆羅門諦，具足不怨害一切眾生、一切行無常、一切法無我三種德行，才是真實的婆羅門，有些外道的婆羅門，自認是最高的種姓，可是他們的行為與他們的種姓是不相稱的，佛陀為了破斥他們的執著，說出一些道理，這段文節錄下來，說明作為一個出家人，應該有這三種婆羅門諦，才名為真實的婆羅門。最後又說只有佛才是真實的婆羅門，又分三科；第一科略標，要略標出非梵志的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，有種姓婆羅門，建立三處為實為諦。然彼種姓諸婆羅門，於此三處住三過失，汙其心故；依第一義，彼皆墮在非梵志數。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，有一類有種姓的婆羅門，建立三種處所為真實為真理。然而出生就是婆羅門的這些人，在這三種處所有三種過失而染污他的心。依究竟最殊勝的道理來說，他們不是真實的修行人，不能說他們是真實的婆羅門。婆羅門有假名婆羅門，種姓婆羅門及第一義婆羅門，他們不是第一義的婆羅門。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、別釋2　辰一、辨三處4　巳一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別的解釋，分二科；第一科辨三處，說明這三處，又分四科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等三處？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪三處？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、為養命，二、為修福，三、安立果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這三處：第一是為了養命，長養生命，為了生存；第二是為了修福；第三是為了生天。這三處外道安立什麼是真實的養命，真實的修福，真實的生天等一大套理論。現在要破斥外道的錯誤。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、釋3　午一、為養命3　未一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科為養命，又分三科；第一科標列，標列出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4464"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為養命者，謂彼種姓諸婆羅門為活命故，於施主前或呪願、或讚美、或序述。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了長養生命，是指出生就是婆羅門的這些人，他們也是去修行當梵志，為了自己能夠活下去，在施主面前持咒然後祈願、或者是讚美施主、或是敘說描述種種事情來求得利養維持生活。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、隨釋3　申一、呪願2　酉一、願除怨敵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋三種養命的方法，分三科；第一科呪願，說明第一種養命的方法是呪願，又分二科；第一科願除怨敵，說呪願施主所有怨敵皆悉消滅等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">呪願者，謂彼種姓諸婆羅門，希求隨一資生具故，往詣王所、或王大臣、或婆羅門、長者、居士、商主等所，矯設呪願：當願汝等所有怨敵皆悉殄滅、橫遭殃禍、摧屈縛錄。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種養命的方法是呪願，是指這些種姓諸婆羅門的外道梵志，為了希求得到活命的資生具，去拜訪國王、大臣、婆羅門、有財富的長老、居士，或者是有錢的商主等，在施主那裡持咒發願，假設說：希望你們所有的怨敵都能夠消滅，慘遭災殃橫禍，而且被摧滅屈伏繫縛等，所有不好的事情都發生在他們身上。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、願常吉祥</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科願常吉祥，說明願常吉祥咒願。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又願汝等所有吉祥常無轉動、不可侵奪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二個咒願：希望你們常常吉祥如意，而且財富地位沒有變動，不被侵損傷害。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、讚美2　酉一、讚害怨敵2　戌一、有力能</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科讚美，說明第二種養命的方法是讚美，分二科；第一科讚害怨敵，讚歎謀害怨敵，又分二科；第一科有力能，讚歎施主有能力傷害怨敵。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">讚美者，為希求故，往到彼所，矯設讚美，言：汝勇健，多諸計策，善害怨敵。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種養命的方法是讚美，是指這些外道婆羅門為希望追求利養，到施主處，假立言詞讚美說：你們是很勇敢、很強健的，你們有很多的計策可以傷害怨家仇敵。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、世希有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科世希有，對於傷害怨敵假興讚美世間難得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於害怨假興讚述，唱言：汝曹如是如是害除怨敵，甚為希有，如汝等輩，世間難得。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　接著對於傷害怨家仇敵，假言讚歎說：你們是這樣子有能力來傷害剷除怨家仇敵，實在是很少見，像你們這種人，真是世間難得的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、讚久興盛</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科讚久興盛，希望讚歎施主財位長久興盛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4465"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於財位久興盛者，矯施讚述，言：諸世間如汝吉祥成就無動，甚為難有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於財位長久興盛的施主，就假立言詞讚歎施主說：在這個世間上，像你們這樣的能夠吉祥成就，這麼多財富地位長久興盛，而且都沒有改變，實在是非常稀少。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、序述2　酉一、序他相好2　戌一、滅敵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科序述，說明第三種養命的方法是序述，分二科；第一科序他相好，敘說施主相好，又分二科；第一科滅敵，敘說施主相好必能滅敵。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">序述者，謂彼為希求故，往到他所，妄興序述；言：汝成就善丈夫相，不久定當一切怨敵皆悉殄滅、橫遭殃禍、摧屈縛錄。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種養命的方法是序述，是指這些外道婆羅門為希望追求利養，到施主處，虛妄的提起話題說：你們成就大丈夫相，所有的一切怨家仇敵，不久一定都能夠消滅、慘遭災殃橫禍，而且被摧滅屈伏繫縛，所有不好的事情都會發生在他們身上。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、吉祥</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科吉祥，序述施主的吉祥相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又若成就如是相者，定當吉祥，無有退轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　並且敘說描述，告訴對方說：你們能夠成就這樣的相貌一定很吉祥，能夠摧伏怨敵等，不會退轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、述自受施</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科述自受施，是敘述唯有自己應當受施。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又如汝等諸親友家、若施主家，常無有餘沙門、婆羅門於中受施執為己有，唯我常得恭敬供養、衣服、飲食、諸臥具等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於類似你們的親友家或施主家，應該不要去布施其他的沙門和婆羅門，不要布施給其他的出家人，應該布施給我。只有我應該常常得到恭敬供養、衣服、飲食、還有諸臥具等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、總結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科總結，總結外道沙門、婆羅門以呪願、讚美、序述三種方法獲得利養，並於其中深生染著。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼由如是方便所獲利養，深生染著、耽嗜、迷悶、堅固、保執而受用之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一類的種姓婆羅門、梵志，由呪願、讚美、序述等種種的方法獲得很多利養，對於所獲得的利養深深染著，耽溺愛好、使自己的心迷失悶著，失去辨別與判斷的能力，不能出離、堅固剛強的保護執持來受用這些衣服飲食臥具湯藥等利養。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、為修福2　未一、別辨相3　申一、殺害眾生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科為修福，三處中的第二處，為了修福，種性婆羅門建立一些錯誤的理論，執為諦實，分二科；第一科別辨相，各別的說明為修福所建立的理論，又分三科；第一科殺害眾生，宣說殺害眾生祭祀能夠得福。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4466"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為修福者，謂彼種姓諸婆羅門，宣說殺害無量眾生，興祠祀福。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些種姓婆羅門，為歡喜修福的施主，宣稱殺害無量眾生來祭祀神廟，可以得到福報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、獲常處果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科獲常處果，宣稱於神廟祭祀修福可以生天。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宣說祠祀、獲常處果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　宣稱透過於神廟祭祀天神而修福，可以生天，獲得常住不變的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》宣說祠祀獲常處果者：謂如害為正法論者，起如是見，立如是論：若於彼祠中呪術為先，害諸生命，若能祀者、若所害者、若諸助伴，如是一切皆得生天。由彼妄計天身是常，是故說言獲常處果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類外道名害為正法論者，生起這樣的見解，安立這樣的言論：若在神廟中先持咒，再殺害豬、羊等來祭祀，這樣做時，能祭祀的人、被殺害的豬羊等、或者幫忙殺豬宰羊的人，這些人畜都可以生天。由於他們虛妄執著天的果報常住不變，永遠不會死，故說祭祀天神可以獲常處果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、攝執我所</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科攝執我所，將供品執為己有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又興祠祀時，召命無量國王、大臣、長者、居士，為欲攝受上妙眾多資生具故。彼既獲已，執為我所，展轉互起陵懱之心。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這些外道發起到神廟祭祀修福時，召集號令無量的國王、大臣、長者、居士，要他們來祭祀。這是為了要拿到很多上等美好的資生具，比如殺豬宰羊就有得吃了，又能拿到很多供品。得到這些供養的物品以後，收下來自己用，就認為是自己的，生起我所的執著，彼此之間又由比較所得供養的勝劣，生起互相欺凌輕視的心念。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、結三失</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結三失，結說他們有三種過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知彼有如是三失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知外道婆羅門為了修福的施主們所建立的理論，有三種心懷染污的過失，第一是殺生的過失，第二是妄執生天為常住不變的果報，第三是執著我我所的過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4467"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》當知彼有如是三失者：謂殺害眾生失、妄計常果失、執我我所失應知。雖為修福，而實非福，是故成失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知外道婆羅門有三種過失，第一是認為殺害眾生祭祀得福，有殺害眾生之過失；第二是妄執祭祀天神可以得常處果，有妄計常果之過失；第三由所獲上妙眾多資生具生起我所執，展轉互起陵懱之心，有執我我所之過失。然為了修福，可是實在得不到福報，不是真實修福，所以成為過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、安立果2　未一、敘彼計</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科安立果，三處中的第三處，安立婆羅門種姓是最殊勝的果報，分二科；第一科敘彼計，說明他們的執著。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">安立果者，謂彼種姓諸婆羅門，說阿素洛身應可殺害，天身是常；唯婆羅門最上種姓，餘姓下劣；廣說乃至諸婆羅門大梵所生，大梵所化，大梵支胤。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　安立果的邪執，是指有一類種姓諸婆羅門，說阿素洛，即阿修羅身應該可以殺害，天身常住不變；唯獨婆羅門是最勝上等的種姓，其他剎帝利、吠舍、首陀羅三種種姓，都是下劣的；他們還有種種的說法，乃至說諸婆羅門是初禪天的最高天大梵天王所生的，大梵天王所變化的，大梵天王的後代。支是指支分；胤是後嗣義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、結得名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結得名，結成得安立果的名稱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼種姓婆羅門作如是計，立如是論，當知是名安立果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　那一類種姓婆羅門作如上所說的執著，安立這樣的言論，認為阿修羅可以殺害的，天身常住不變，唯獨婆羅門是最勝上等的種姓，名安立果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》唯婆羅門最上種姓等者：謂如妄計最勝論者，起如是見，立如是論：婆羅門是最勝種類，剎帝利等是下劣種類；婆羅門是白淨色類，餘種是黑穢色類；婆羅門種可得清淨，非餘種類；諸婆羅門是梵王子，從大梵王口腹所生，從梵所出，梵所變化，梵王體胤。如有尋有伺地敘破彼計應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/07.htm#43821:5084">陵本七卷十二頁519</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一種名妄計最勝論者，生起這樣的見地，安立這樣的言論：婆羅門是最殊勝的種類，其他三種剎帝利、吠舍、及首陀羅都是下劣的種類。婆羅門屬於白色、清淨色類的人，其他種姓的人黑皮膚屬於黑色污穢色類的人。婆羅門種姓的人可以得到清淨，其他種姓的人都不能得到清淨。諸婆羅門種姓的人是大梵王的孩子，從大梵王的口，或者是肚子裡面生出來，從梵王所出，梵王所變化，是梵王的後嗣。如〈本地分‧有尋有伺地〉卷7，212頁所敘述破彼外道所執，應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是種姓婆羅門，於此三處猛利取執，隨興言論：唯此是實是諦，餘并愚妄。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些婆羅門種姓，在為了養命、為了修福、為安立果三個處所，產生強大猛盛的見取執著，並且還宣說種種言論，認為只有這樣的理論是真實是真理，其它的道理都是愚痴虛妄的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、顯三失4　巳一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯三失，顯示外道於此三處有三種過失，分四科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4468"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等名為由三過失染汙其心？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼樣的理由說有三種過失會染污他的心？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂語言過失、憍慢過失、勝解過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了養命、為修福、為安立果有三種過失，第一是語言過失，第二是憍慢過失，第三是勝解過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、釋3　午一、語言過失</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科語言過失，說明由三處發出語業成語言過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若即於此三處邪語業轉，當知是名語言過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若在養命、修福、及安立果三處，有不正確的語業生起，是名為語言過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、憍慢過失</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科憍慢過失，說明由三處與人校量高下，成憍慢的過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若復於此三處施設建立，及隨發起不正言論方比於他，謂己為勝、或等、或劣，當知是名憍慢過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若在養命、修福及安立果三處施設建立種種方便，又發起不正當的言論，與他人校量高下，認為自己是殊勝的，或者認為是與他人相等，或者是比他人只差一點，都名為憍慢過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、勝解過失</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科勝解過失，說明由三處不觀得失，成勝解過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若復於此三處不觀得失，一向信受；雖遇諸佛及佛弟子正教誨時，於處非處不能正住，於遍分別不能正住，</span></strong></span></span></p>
