<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果對於養命、修福、還有安立果這三處，不觀察它的功德過失，不正確的去認識他，只是道聽塗說，就一向信受的話，雖然遇到佛及佛弟子，教導正法，於合因果道理之處，如善因得樂果，惡因得苦果，及不合因果道理之非處，如殺生祭祀無罪且可生天等，沒有正確智慧安住在真理上，對於所有緣起法三性差別，虛妄與真實等，都不能正確認識安住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於遍分別不能正住者：謂於圓成實相、依他起相、遍計所執相諸法安立，不能如理而思惟故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於徧分別不能正住，是指對佛於安立諸法的圓成實相的我法二空真如，諸法的唯識性；依他因緣所生的法相，諸法的唯識相；徧計所執相，周徧計度執著的名言相，不能如佛所說的正理來思惟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4469"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於諸正行不能正住，於智者論不能正住，當知是名勝解過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於聞思修、戒定慧等正行不能正住；對於佛菩薩等聖人所說的道理不能安住，稱為勝解過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於智者論不能正住者：若所立論不違聖言，能治雜染，不違法相，名智者論。不依此生法住智故，名不能住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於智者論不能正住，是指所安立的言論，不違背佛說的道理，能夠對治惑業苦的雜染，不違背諸法的實相，名為智者論。不能依佛所說無倒而知，稱為不能住。佛說不得法住智，不能得涅槃智。法住智是對於佛法正確理解的智慧，涅槃智是證悟的智慧，外道於三處有三種過失，有邪勝解、語言、及憍慢等過失，不能有正行，不但沒有法住智，更遑論得涅槃智了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此三過失，當知皆是惡見所起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這三種過失都是邪惡的知見所引起的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、結攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結攝，結論歸納住三處成就三種過失，非梵志數。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="51283:43843"></a>若有住此三處，成就三種過失，雖是種姓諸婆羅門，依第一義，彼皆墮在非梵志數。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果有人住在養命、修福、及安立果這三處，成就語言、憍慢、勝解三種過失，雖然他天生是婆羅門種姓，可是依第一義最殊勝的道理來說，他們不能算是有清淨心的修行人，不是真實的婆羅門。梵是指清淨，志是心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、顯自3　卯一、略標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯自，顯出佛法中第一義婆羅門的道理，分三科；第一科略標，要略標出第一義婆羅門數。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若有建立三處為諦為實，又於三處無三過失染汙其心，彼雖非種姓婆羅門，然墮第一義婆羅門數。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，有建立三處是真實、是真理，又於三處沒有語言、憍慢、勝解三種過失，雖然不是婆羅門種姓出身，也是屬於第一義婆羅門之類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、別辨2　辰一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別辨，各別的說明什麼是三處，分二科；第一科徵，提問什麼是無三過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等三處？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪三處？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、釋2　巳一、舉初處2　午一、標所說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉初處，先舉第一處，又分二科；第一科標所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4470"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂不應害一切眾生，是名初處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不應傷害、殺害一切眾生，是佛教所建立的初處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、顯離過3　未一、無語言過</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯離過，顯示建立初處遠離三種過失，分三科；第一科無語言過，說明於初處無語言過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此所說處，唯諦唯實，無有虛妄。是故於此初處，無語言過失染汙其心。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一處不應殺害一切眾生，這樣的說法是真理，是真實的，完全沒有語言的過失來染污他的內心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、無憍慢過</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無憍慢過，說明於初處無憍慢過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又彼於是處，不由諦實言論方比於他，謂己為勝、若等、若劣。是故彼於此處，無憍慢過失染汙其心。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又於不應殺害一切眾生之處，不因為自己安立的真實言論來與他人比較，認為自己勝過他人，或與他人相等，或是比他人只差少分，這些心情都沒有。故在此初處，沒有憍慢的過失來染污他的內心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又彼於是處等者：此中處言，謂即初處，下皆準知。由依不應害一切眾生而為論故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文中的處，是指初處，下文都準照此初處解釋可知。因為初處是依不應傷害一切眾生而為說，所以沒有語言、憍慢、及勝解等過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、無勝解過2　申一、辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無勝解過，分二科；第一科辨，說明於初處無勝解過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又彼於此處審觀得失，觀彼所緣能增善法。又能攝益身心無罪現法樂住，於諸有情多住慈想，晝夜修學；又於此處非信他行，內自正覺為諦為實，然於諦實不妄執著。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又行者在不傷害一切眾生之處，詳細的觀察功德、過失，觀察所緣不傷害一切眾生的道理，能夠增長善法，助益身體健康，心情安寧，沒有罪過，使現在的生命體安樂而住，對於諸多有情多分安住慈心的想法，日夜不停的修習慈心觀；又於不應殺害一切眾生的道理，不是由於相信他人所說而行，而是從內心裡面自己覺悟的，這是真理，而且是事實，對於這個真理事實，不虛妄執著，所以沒有勝解的過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又於此處非信他行者：謂於不害眾生處獲得無漏律儀，終不故思違越所學，乃至傍生亦不害命故。如是律儀自內所證，非緣於他，是名非信他行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又於此處非信他行，是指對於不傷害眾生處獲得無漏戒體，成就聖所愛戒，有無漏戒的功德。不會故意想要違背所學的戒律，乃至不傷害畜生的生命。這種無漏戒體，是內心證得無分別智以後，自己覺悟到，不應該殺害一切眾生，不是由於他人告訴他不要殺害眾生，才不殺害眾生。由此可見，不殺害一切有情，修慈無量心，也是一種解脫門。在《大毘婆沙論》卷77，400頁裡面，也有說到這一大段，認為安立不應害一切有情這個道理，屬於修空解脫門，修空解脫門成功時，安立出來的理論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4471"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故當知，彼於此處，無勝解過失染汙其心。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所以應當了知，在不殺害一切眾生處所，在思想上沒有錯誤的認識，無勝解過失染污他的心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、例餘處2　午一、例同</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘處，分二科；第一科例同，推例其他二處道理如前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是一切行無常，是名第二處。餘如前說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一切行無常，是佛教所安立的第二處。其他的如前不應殺害一切眾生所說，沒有語言過失、沒有憍慢過失、沒有勝解過失。第二處一切行無常，在《大毘婆沙論》卷77，400頁裡面，安立成無相解脫門，認為「諸有集法皆有滅法」，凡積聚的法，都會消滅，都是剎那無常的，由這樣觀想可以證得無相解脫門。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》餘如前說者：謂如初處離三過失應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　餘如前說，是指如初處不應殺害一切眾生所說，遠離語言、憍慢、及勝解三種過失，應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一切法無我，是名第三處。餘如前說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一切法無我，是佛教安立的第三處，其他的如前不應殺害一切眾生所說，沒有三種過失。第三處一切法無我，在《大毘婆沙論》裡面安立成無願解脫門，論上說：「我非彼所有，彼非我所有，」我不是五蘊所有，如此五蘊不是我所有，這樣觀想可以證得無願解脫門，以三解脫門來破斥對方的邪論。本論沒有明顯的說出來，只有在不應殺害一切眾生，於安住慈想，修慈心觀；於一切行無常，安住無常想，修生滅觀，於一切法無我，安住無我我所想，修無我觀，與《大毘婆沙論》不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、顯別2　未一、於第二諦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯別，顯示第二處及第三處與初處的差別，分二科；第一科於第二諦，說明於第二諦住生滅觀晝夜修學。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中差別者，於第二諦，應言於一切行多住生滅觀，晝夜修學。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二處一切行無常與初處不應殺害一切眾生修慈心觀不同處是：行者多住生滅觀，觀察有為法剎那生滅，日夜精進修學。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、於第三諦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於第三諦，說明於第三諦，住無我我所想，晝夜修學。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於第三諦，應言於一切法多住無我我所想，晝夜修學。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於第三諦一切法無我，應該多修一切法無我我所想，觀察有為、無為諸法無我，也不是我所有，日夜精進修學。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="55p4472"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、總結2　辰一、明勝義攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科總結，分二科；第一科明勝義攝，說明於三處無三過失，屬第一義婆羅門數。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有於此三處無三過失染汙其心，彼雖非種姓婆羅門，然墮第一義婆羅門數。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若有行者於：一、不應害一切眾生，二、一切行無常，三、一切法無我這三處，沒有語言、憍慢、及勝解等三種過失染汙他的心，這類行者雖然不是種姓婆羅門，然而卻屬於與勝義諦相應的第一義婆羅門之類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、為佛知見</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科為佛知見，說明不應殺生等三處為佛的知見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是三處成婆羅門諦實之法，離三過失，唯有如來是真覺者。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是不應殺害一切眾生、一切行無常、一切法無我這三處，是成為婆羅門的真理、真實之法。遠離語言、憍慢及、勝解三種過失，只有佛才是真正的覺悟的人，才能如此善巧安立。這裡特別標出，只有佛才是真正的婆羅門、第一義婆羅門、圓滿的婆羅門。這樣就將己方安立的三處顯出來，破斥外道的三處。真正的婆羅門的三諦，是佛所安立的：不應殺害一切眾生、一切行無常、還有一切法無我。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第五十五</span></strong></span></span><br />
&nbsp;</p>

<div id="gtx-trans" style="border-radius:5px; border:1px solid #dcdcdc; padding:3px; text-align:start; width:19px">&nbsp;</div>
